# alsace
world_stage_alsace_category = {
	decision_theater_alsace_reinforce = {
		icon = theater_reinforce
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_alsace }
		available = {
			if = { limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } }  has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_alsace_retreat
						#has_decision = decision_theater_alsace_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_alsace_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_alsace_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_5_or_10_power_cost
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
				set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.ENG_strength_alsace = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.FRA_strength_alsace = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.SOV_strength_alsace = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_sov = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.USA_strength_alsace = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.NET_strength_alsace = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 7 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.PRT_strength_alsace = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.CHI_strength_alsace = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				add_to_variable = { global.GER_strength_alsace = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = reinforcements_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_alsace_retreat = {
		icon = theater_retreat
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_alsace }
		available = {
			has_strength_alsace = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_alsace_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_alsace_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_alsace_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_alsace_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.ENG_strength_alsace }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.ENG_strength_alsace = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.FRA_strength_alsace }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.FRA_strength_alsace = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.SOV_strength_alsace }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_sov = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.SOV_strength_alsace = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.USA_strength_alsace }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.USA_strength_alsace = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.NET_strength_alsace }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.NET_strength_alsace = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 7 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.PRT_strength_alsace }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.PRT_strength_alsace = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.CHI_strength_alsace }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.CHI_strength_alsace = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.GER_strength_alsace }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.GER_strength_alsace = trickleback_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_alsace_defend = {
		icon = theater_defend
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_alsace
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_alsace = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_alsace_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_alsace_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_alsace_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_alsace_offensive }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = allies_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_alsace_bonus > 0 }
				}
			} else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = axis_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_alsace_bonus > 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_alsace_bonus > 50 } }
					add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_alsace_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_alsace_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.ALLIES_strength_alsace_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			} else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_alsace_bonus > 50 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_alsace_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_alsace_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_alsace_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_alsace_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_alsace
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_alsace = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_alsace_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_alsace_defend
						#has_decision = decision_theater_alsace_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_alsace_reinforce }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }
			if = { limit = { has_20_strength_alsace = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_alsace = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_alsace_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_alsace } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_alsace_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_alsace } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_alsace_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_alsace } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_alsace_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_alsace } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_alsace_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_alsace } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_alsace_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_alsace } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
# france
world_stage_france_category = {
	decision_theater_france_reinforce = {
		icon = theater_reinforce
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_france }
		available = {
			if = { limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }

			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }

				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = reinforcements_value }

		}
	}

		icon = theater_defend

		}
		available = {

					tooltip = axis_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_france_bonus > 0 }

		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost

			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_france_bonus > 50 } }

				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_france_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.ALLIES_strength_france_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }

				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_france_bonus > 50 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_france_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_france_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_france_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_france_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_france
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_france = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_france_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_france_defend
						#has_decision = decision_theater_france_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_france_reinforce }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }
			if = { limit = { has_20_strength_france = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_france = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_france_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_france } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_france_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_france } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_france_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_france } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_france_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_france } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_france_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_france } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_france_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_france } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

# westphalia
world_stage_westphalia_category = {
	decision_theater_westphalia_reinforce = {
		icon = theater_reinforce
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_westphalia }
		available = {
			if = { limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } }  has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_westphalia_retreat
						#has_decision = decision_theater_westphalia_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_westphalia_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_westphalia_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_5_or_10_power_cost
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
				set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.ENG_strength_westphalia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.FRA_strength_westphalia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.SOV_strength_westphalia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_sov = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.USA_strength_westphalia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.NET_strength_westphalia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 7 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.PRT_strength_westphalia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.CHI_strength_westphalia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				add_to_variable = { global.GER_strength_westphalia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = reinforcements_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_westphalia_retreat = {
		icon = theater_retreat
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_westphalia }
		available = {
			has_strength_westphalia = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_westphalia_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_westphalia_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_westphalia_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_westphalia_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.ENG_strength_westphalia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.ENG_strength_westphalia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.FRA_strength_westphalia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.FRA_strength_westphalia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.SOV_strength_westphalia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }

			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.USA_strength_westphalia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }

				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.USA_strength_westphalia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.NET_strength_westphalia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.NET_strength_westphalia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 7 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.PRT_strength_westphalia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.PRT_strength_westphalia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.CHI_strength_westphalia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.CHI_strength_westphalia = trickleback_value }

				subtract_from_variable = { global.GER_strength_westphalia = trickleback_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_westphalia_defend = {
		icon = theater_defend
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_westphalia
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_westphalia = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {

						has_decision = decision_theater_westphalia_offensive }

				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }

					tooltip = allies_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_westphalia_bonus > 0 }
				}
			} else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = axis_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_westphalia_bonus > 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_westphalia_bonus > 50 } }
					add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_westphalia_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_westphalia_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.ALLIES_strength_westphalia_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			} else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_westphalia_bonus > 50 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_westphalia_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_westphalia_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_westphalia_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_westphalia_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_westphalia
		}
		available = {

			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }

				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_westphalia = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {

				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_westphalia_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_westphalia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_westphalia_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_westphalia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_westphalia_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_westphalia } }
				}

					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_westphalia_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_westphalia } }

				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.CHI_strength_germany = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.GER_strength_germany }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.GER_strength_germany = trickleback_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_germany_defend = {
		icon = theater_defend
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_germany
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_germany = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_germany_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_germany_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_germany_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_germany_offensive }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = allies_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_germany_bonus > 0 }
				}
			} else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = axis_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_germany_bonus > 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_germany_bonus > 50 } }
					add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_germany_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_germany_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.ALLIES_strength_germany_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			} else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_germany_bonus > 50 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_germany_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_germany_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_germany_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_germany_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_germany
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_germany = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_germany_retreat

			}

		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }
			if = { limit = { has_20_strength_germany = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_germany = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_germany_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_germany } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_germany_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_germany } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_germany_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_germany } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_germany_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_germany } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_germany_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_germany } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_germany_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_germany } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

world_stage_poland_category = {
	decision_theater_poland_reinforce = {
		icon = theater_reinforce
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_poland }
		available = {
			if = { limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } }  has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_poland_retreat
						#has_decision = decision_theater_poland_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_poland_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_poland_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_5_or_10_power_cost
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
				set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.ENG_strength_poland = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }

				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.ENG_strength_belarus = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.FRA_strength_belarus }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.FRA_strength_belarus = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.SOV_strength_belarus }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_sov = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.SOV_strength_belarus = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.USA_strength_belarus }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.USA_strength_belarus = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.NET_strength_belarus }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.NET_strength_belarus = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 7 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.PRT_strength_belarus }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.PRT_strength_belarus = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.CHI_strength_belarus }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.CHI_strength_belarus = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.GER_strength_belarus }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.GER_strength_belarus = trickleback_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_belarus_defend = {
		icon = theater_defend
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_belarus
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_belarus = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_belarus_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_belarus_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_belarus_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_belarus_offensive }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = allies_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_belarus_bonus > 0 }
				}
			} else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = axis_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_belarus_bonus > 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_belarus_bonus > 50 } }
					add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_belarus_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_belarus_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.ALLIES_strength_belarus_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			} else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_belarus_bonus > 50 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_belarus_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_belarus_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_belarus_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_belarus_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_belarus
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_belarus = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_belarus_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_belarus_defend
						#has_decision = decision_theater_belarus_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_belarus_reinforce }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }
			if = { limit = { has_20_strength_belarus = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_belarus = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_belarus_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_belarus } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_belarus_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_belarus } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_belarus_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_belarus } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_belarus_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_belarus } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_belarus_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_belarus } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_belarus_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_belarus } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	decision_theater_smolensk_reinforce = {
		icon = theater_reinforce
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_smolensk }
		available = {
			if = { limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } }  has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater

		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
				set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.ENG_strength_smolensk = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }

			}

				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.FRA_strength_russia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.SOV_strength_russia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }

				add_to_variable = { global.GER_strength_russia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = reinforcements_value }

		}

	decision_theater_russia_retreat = {
		icon = theater_retreat
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_russia }
		available = {
			has_strength_russia = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_russia_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_russia_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_russia_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_russia_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.ENG_strength_russia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.ENG_strength_russia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.FRA_strength_russia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.FRA_strength_russia = trickleback_value }
			}

				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }

				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }

				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.USA_strength_russia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.USA_strength_russia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.NET_strength_russia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }

		}

				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_russia_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_russia_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_russia_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_russia_offensive }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = allies_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_russia_bonus > 0 }
				}
			} else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = axis_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_russia_bonus > 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_russia_bonus > 50 } }
					add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_russia_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_russia_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.ALLIES_strength_russia_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			} else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_russia_bonus > 50 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_russia_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_russia_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_russia_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_russia_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_russia
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_russia = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_russia_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_russia_defend
						#has_decision = decision_theater_russia_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_russia_reinforce }
			}

		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }
			if = { limit = { has_20_strength_russia = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_russia = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_russia_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_russia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_russia_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_russia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_russia_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_russia } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_russia_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_russia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_russia_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_russia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_russia_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_russia } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_urals_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_urals } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_urals_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_urals } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_urals_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_urals } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_urals_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_urals } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_urals_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_urals } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_urals_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_urals } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

world_stage_siberia_category = {
	decision_theater_siberia_reinforce = {
		icon = theater_reinforce
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_siberia }
		available = {
			if = { limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } }  has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_siberia_retreat
						#has_decision = decision_theater_siberia_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_siberia_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_siberia_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_5_or_10_power_cost
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
				set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.ENG_strength_siberia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.FRA_strength_siberia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.SOV_strength_siberia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_sov = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.USA_strength_siberia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.NET_strength_siberia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 7 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.PRT_strength_siberia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.CHI_strength_siberia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				add_to_variable = { global.GER_strength_siberia = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = reinforcements_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_siberia_retreat = {
		icon = theater_retreat
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_siberia }
		available = {
			has_strength_siberia = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_siberia_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_siberia_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_siberia_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_siberia_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.ENG_strength_siberia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.ENG_strength_siberia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.FRA_strength_siberia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.FRA_strength_siberia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.SOV_strength_siberia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value

				subtract_from_variable = { global.SOV_strength_siberia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.USA_strength_siberia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.USA_strength_siberia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.NET_strength_siberia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.NET_strength_siberia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 7 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.PRT_strength_siberia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.PRT_strength_siberia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.CHI_strength_siberia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.CHI_strength_siberia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.GER_strength_siberia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.GER_strength_siberia = trickleback_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_siberia_defend = {
		icon = theater_defend
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_siberia
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_siberia = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_siberia_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_siberia_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_siberia_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_siberia_offensive }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = allies_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_siberia_bonus > 0 }
				}
			} else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = axis_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_siberia_bonus > 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_siberia_bonus > 50 } }
					add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_siberia_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_siberia_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.ALLIES_strength_siberia_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			} else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_siberia_bonus > 50 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_siberia_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_siberia_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_siberia_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_siberia_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_siberia
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_siberia = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_siberia_retreat

						has_decision = decision_theater_siberia_reinforce }
			}

		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }
			if = { limit = { has_20_strength_siberia = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_siberia = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_siberia_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_siberia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_siberia_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_siberia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_siberia_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_siberia } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_siberia_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_siberia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_siberia_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_siberia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_siberia_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_siberia } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

					check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_mongolia_bonus > 0 }
				}
			} else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = axis_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_mongolia_bonus > 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_mongolia_bonus > 50 } }
					add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_mongolia_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_mongolia_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.ALLIES_strength_mongolia_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			} else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_mongolia_bonus > 50 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_mongolia_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_mongolia_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_mongolia_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_mongolia_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_mongolia
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_mongolia = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_mongolia_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_mongolia_defend
						#has_decision = decision_theater_mongolia_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_mongolia_reinforce }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }
			if = { limit = { has_20_strength_mongolia = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_mongolia = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_mongolia_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_mongolia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_mongolia_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_mongolia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_mongolia_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_mongolia } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_mongolia_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_mongolia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_mongolia_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_mongolia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_mongolia_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_mongolia } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

# tibet
world_stage_tibet_category = {
	decision_theater_tibet_reinforce = {
		icon = theater_reinforce
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_tibet }
		available = {
			if = { limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } }  has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_tibet_retreat
						#has_decision = decision_theater_tibet_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_tibet_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_tibet_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_5_or_10_power_cost
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
				set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.ENG_strength_tibet = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.FRA_strength_tibet = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.SOV_strength_tibet = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_sov = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.USA_strength_tibet = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.NET_strength_tibet = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 7 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.PRT_strength_tibet = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.CHI_strength_tibet = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				add_to_variable = { global.GER_strength_tibet = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = reinforcements_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_tibet_retreat = {
		icon = theater_retreat
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_tibet }
		available = {
			has_strength_tibet = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_tibet_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_tibet_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_tibet_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_tibet_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.ENG_strength_tibet }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.ENG_strength_tibet = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.FRA_strength_tibet }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.FRA_strength_tibet = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.SOV_strength_tibet }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }

				subtract_from_variable = { global.SOV_strength_tibet = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.USA_strength_tibet }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.USA_strength_tibet = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.NET_strength_tibet }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }

			if = {

				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.CHI_strength_tibet }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.USA_strength_guanxi }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.USA_strength_guanxi = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.NET_strength_guanxi }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.NET_strength_guanxi = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 7 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.PRT_strength_guanxi }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.PRT_strength_guanxi = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.CHI_strength_guanxi }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.CHI_strength_guanxi = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.GER_strength_guanxi }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.GER_strength_guanxi = trickleback_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_guanxi_defend = {
		icon = theater_defend
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_guanxi
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_guanxi = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_guanxi_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_guanxi_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_guanxi_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_guanxi_offensive }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = allies_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_guanxi_bonus > 0 }
				}
			} else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = axis_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_guanxi_bonus > 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_guanxi_bonus > 50 } }
					add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_guanxi_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_guanxi_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.ALLIES_strength_guanxi_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			} else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_guanxi_bonus > 50 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_guanxi_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_guanxi_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_guanxi_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_guanxi_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_guanxi
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_guanxi = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_guanxi_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_guanxi_defend
						#has_decision = decision_theater_guanxi_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_guanxi_reinforce }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }
			if = { limit = { has_20_strength_guanxi = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_guanxi = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_guanxi_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_guanxi } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_guanxi_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_guanxi } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_guanxi_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_guanxi } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_guanxi_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_guanxi } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_guanxi_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_guanxi } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_guanxi_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_guanxi } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

world_stage_china_category = {
	decision_theater_china_reinforce = {
		icon = theater_reinforce
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_china }
		available = {
			if = { limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } }  has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_china_retreat
						#has_decision = decision_theater_china_supply

		}

		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
				set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.ENG_strength_china = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = reinforcements_value }
			}

				add_to_variable = { global.CHI_strength_bengal = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				add_to_variable = { global.GER_strength_bengal = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = reinforcements_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_bengal_retreat = {
		icon = theater_retreat
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_bengal }
		available = {
			has_strength_bengal = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_bengal_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_bengal_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_bengal_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_bengal_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.ENG_strength_bengal }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.ENG_strength_bengal = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.FRA_strength_bengal }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.FRA_strength_bengal = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.SOV_strength_bengal }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
