			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.USA_strength_bengal }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.USA_strength_bengal = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.NET_strength_bengal }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }

				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }

				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }

						has_decision = decision_theater_bengal_reinforce

						has_decision = decision_theater_bengal_offensive }

				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = allies_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_bengal_bonus > 0 }
				}
			} else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = axis_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_bengal_bonus > 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_bengal_bonus > 50 } }
					add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_bengal_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_bengal_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.ALLIES_strength_bengal_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			} else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_bengal_bonus > 50 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_bengal_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_bengal_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_bengal_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_bengal_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_bengal
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_bengal = yes

		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }
			if = { limit = { has_20_strength_bengal = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_bengal = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_bengal_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_bengal } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_bengal_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_bengal } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_bengal_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_bengal } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_bengal_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_bengal } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_bengal_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_bengal } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_bengal_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_bengal } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		available = {
			if = { limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } }  has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_philipines_retreat
						#has_decision = decision_theater_philipines_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_philipines_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_philipines_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_5_or_10_power_cost
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
				set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.ENG_strength_philipines = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.FRA_strength_philipines = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.SOV_strength_philipines = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_sov = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.USA_strength_philipines = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.NET_strength_philipines = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 7 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.PRT_strength_philipines = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.CHI_strength_philipines = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				add_to_variable = { global.GER_strength_philipines = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = reinforcements_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_philipines_retreat = {
		icon = theater_retreat
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_philipines }
		available = {
			has_strength_philipines = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_philipines_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_philipines_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_philipines_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_philipines_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.ENG_strength_philipines }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.ENG_strength_philipines = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.FRA_strength_philipines }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.FRA_strength_philipines = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.SOV_strength_philipines }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_sov = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.SOV_strength_philipines = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.USA_strength_philipines }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.USA_strength_philipines = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.NET_strength_philipines }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.NET_strength_philipines = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 7 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.PRT_strength_philipines }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }

			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.CHI_strength_philipines }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }

				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }

	decision_theater_philipines_defend = {
		icon = theater_defend
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_philipines
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_philipines = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_philipines_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_philipines_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_philipines_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_philipines_offensive }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = allies_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_philipines_bonus > 0 }
				}
			} else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = axis_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_philipines_bonus > 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_philipines_bonus > 50 } }
					add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_philipines_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_philipines_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.ALLIES_strength_philipines_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			} else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_philipines_bonus > 50 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_philipines_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_philipines_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_philipines_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_philipines_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_philipines
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_philipines = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_philipines_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_philipines_defend
						#has_decision = decision_theater_philipines_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_philipines_reinforce }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }
			if = { limit = { has_20_strength_philipines = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_philipines = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_philipines_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_philipines } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_philipines_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_philipines } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_philipines_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_philipines } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_philipines_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_philipines } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_philipines_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_philipines } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_philipines_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_philipines } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_indies_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_indies_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_indies_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_indies_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_indies
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_indies = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_indies_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_indies_defend
						#has_decision = decision_theater_indies_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_indies_reinforce }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }
			if = { limit = { has_20_strength_indies = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_indies = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_indies_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_indies } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_indies_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_indies } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_indies_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_indies } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_indies_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_indies } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_indies_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_indies } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_indies_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_indies } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

# england
world_stage_england_category = {
	decision_theater_england_reinforce = {
		icon = theater_reinforce
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_england }
		available = {
			if = { limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } }  has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_england_retreat
						#has_decision = decision_theater_england_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_england_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_england_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_5_or_10_power_cost
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
				set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.ENG_strength_england = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.FRA_strength_england = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.SOV_strength_england = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_sov = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.USA_strength_england = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = reinforcements_value }
			}

				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.NET_strength_england = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = reinforcements_value }

				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 7 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.PRT_strength_england = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.CHI_strength_england = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				add_to_variable = { global.GER_strength_england = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = reinforcements_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_england_retreat = {
		icon = theater_retreat
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_england }
		available = {
			has_strength_england = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_england_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_england_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_england_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_england_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.ENG_strength_england }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.ENG_strength_england = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.FRA_strength_england }

				subtract_from_variable = { global.FRA_strength_england = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.SOV_strength_england }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }

			if = {

				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.USA_strength_england = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.NET_strength_england }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value

				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value

			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.CHI_strength_england }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value

					add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_england_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_england_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}

			} else = {

					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_england_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_england_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_england_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}

				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }

			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_england = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }

				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.CHI_strength_normandy }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.CHI_strength_normandy = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.GER_strength_normandy }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.GER_strength_normandy = trickleback_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_normandy_defend = {
		icon = theater_defend
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_normandy
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_normandy = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_normandy_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_normandy_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_normandy_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_normandy_offensive }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = allies_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_normandy_bonus > 0 }
				}
			} else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = axis_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_normandy_bonus > 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_normandy_bonus > 50 } }
					add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_normandy_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_normandy_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.ALLIES_strength_normandy_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			} else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_normandy_bonus > 50 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_normandy_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_normandy_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_normandy_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_normandy_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_normandy
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_normandy = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_normandy_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_normandy_defend

						has_decision = decision_theater_normandy_reinforce }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }
			if = { limit = { has_20_strength_normandy = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_normandy = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_normandy_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_normandy } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_normandy_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_normandy } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_normandy_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_normandy } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_normandy_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_normandy } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_normandy_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_normandy } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_normandy_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_normandy } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.ENG_strength_lybia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.FRA_strength_lybia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.FRA_strength_lybia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.SOV_strength_lybia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_sov = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.SOV_strength_lybia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.USA_strength_lybia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.USA_strength_lybia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.NET_strength_lybia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.NET_strength_lybia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 7 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.PRT_strength_lybia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.PRT_strength_lybia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.CHI_strength_lybia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.CHI_strength_lybia = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.GER_strength_lybia }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value

				subtract_from_variable = { global.GER_strength_lybia = trickleback_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_lybia_defend = {
		icon = theater_defend
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_lybia
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_lybia = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_lybia_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_lybia_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_lybia_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_lybia_offensive }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = allies_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_lybia_bonus > 0 }
				}
			} else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = axis_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_lybia_bonus > 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_lybia_bonus > 50 } }
					add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_lybia_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_lybia_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.ALLIES_strength_lybia_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			} else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_lybia_bonus > 50 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_lybia_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_lybia_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_lybia_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_lybia_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_lybia
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_lybia = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_lybia_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_lybia_defend
						#has_decision = decision_theater_lybia_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_lybia_reinforce }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }
			if = { limit = { has_20_strength_lybia = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_lybia = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_lybia_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_lybia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_lybia_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_lybia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_lybia_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_lybia } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_lybia_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_lybia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_lybia_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_lybia } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_lybia_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_lybia } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			if = { limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }

			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.SOV_strength_alpes = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_sov = reinforcements_value }
			}

				add_to_variable = { global.USA_strength_alpes = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }

				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = reinforcements_value }

				add_to_variable = { global.CHI_strength_alpes = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				add_to_variable = { global.GER_strength_alpes = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = reinforcements_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_alpes_retreat = {
		icon = theater_retreat
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_alpes }
		available = {
			has_strength_alpes = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_alpes_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_alpes_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_alpes_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_alpes_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.ENG_strength_alpes }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.ENG_strength_alpes = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.FRA_strength_alpes }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.FRA_strength_alpes = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.SOV_strength_alpes }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_sov = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.SOV_strength_alpes = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.USA_strength_alpes }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.USA_strength_alpes = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.NET_strength_alpes }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.NET_strength_alpes = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 7 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.PRT_strength_alpes }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.PRT_strength_alpes = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.CHI_strength_alpes }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }

		icon = theater_defend
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_alpes
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_alpes = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_alpes_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_alpes_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_alpes_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_alpes_offensive }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = allies_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_alpes_bonus > 0 }
				}
			} else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = axis_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_alpes_bonus > 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_alpes_bonus > 50 } }
					add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_alpes_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_alpes_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.ALLIES_strength_alpes_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			} else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_alpes_bonus > 50 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_alpes_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_alpes_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_alpes_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_alpes_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_alpes
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_alpes = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_alpes_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_alpes_defend

						has_decision = decision_theater_alpes_reinforce }

		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }
			if = { limit = { has_20_strength_alpes = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_alpes = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_alpes_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_alpes } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_alpes_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_alpes } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_alpes_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_alpes } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_alpes_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_alpes } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_alpes_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_alpes } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_alpes_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_alpes } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_italy_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_italy } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_italy_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_italy } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_italy_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_italy } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_italy_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_italy } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_italy_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_italy } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_italy_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_italy } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

# sicily
world_stage_sicily_category = {
	decision_theater_sicily_reinforce = {
		icon = theater_reinforce
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_sicily }
		available = {
			if = { limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes } }  has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_sicily_retreat
						#has_decision = decision_theater_sicily_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_sicily_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_sicily_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_5 = yes }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_5_or_10_power_cost
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_power_SELF_10 = yes }
				set_temp_variable = { reinforcements_value = 10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.ENG_strength_sicily = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.FRA_strength_sicily = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.SOV_strength_sicily = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_sov = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.USA_strength_sicily = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.NET_strength_sicily = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 7 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.PRT_strength_sicily = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				add_to_variable = { global.CHI_strength_sicily = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = reinforcements_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				add_to_variable = { global.GER_strength_sicily = reinforcements_value tooltip = world_stage_deploy_power_here }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.world_stage_power_ger = reinforcements_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_sicily_retreat = {
		icon = theater_retreat
		visible = {	has_country_flag = can_play_sicily }
		available = {
			has_strength_sicily = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_sicily_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_sicily_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_sicily_defend
						has_decision = decision_theater_sicily_offensive }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 2 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.ENG_strength_sicily }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_eng = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.ENG_strength_sicily = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 3 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.FRA_strength_sicily }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_fra = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.FRA_strength_sicily = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 4 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.SOV_strength_sicily }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_sov = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.SOV_strength_sicily = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 5 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.USA_strength_sicily }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_usa = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.USA_strength_sicily = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 6 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.NET_strength_sicily }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_NET = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.NET_strength_sicily = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 7 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.PRT_strength_sicily }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_prt = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.PRT_strength_sicily = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 8 } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.CHI_strength_sicily }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = trickleback_value
				add_to_variable = { global.world_stage_power_chi = trickleback_value tooltip = strength_trickleback_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { global.CHI_strength_sicily = trickleback_value }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 9 } check_variable = { world_stage_metropolis = 10 } } }
				set_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = global.GER_strength_sicily }
				divide_temp_variable = { trickleback_value = 2 }

				subtract_from_variable = { global.GER_strength_sicily = trickleback_value }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_sicily_defend = {
		icon = theater_defend
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_sicily
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_sicily = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_sicily_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_sicily_reinforce
						#has_decision = decision_theater_sicily_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_sicily_offensive }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = allies_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_sicily_bonus > 0 }
				}
			} else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = axis_have_strategic_advantage
					check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_sicily_bonus > 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_sicily_bonus > 50 } }
					add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_sicily_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_sicily_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.ALLIES_strength_sicily_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			} else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_sicily_bonus > 50 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_sicily_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_sicily_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_sicily_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_sicily_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_sicily
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_sicily = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_sicily_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_sicily_defend
						#has_decision = decision_theater_sicily_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_sicily_reinforce }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }
			if = { limit = { has_20_strength_sicily = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_sicily = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_sicily_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_sicily } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_sicily_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_sicily } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_sicily_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_sicily } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_sicily_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_sicily } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_sicily_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_sicily } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_sicily_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_sicily } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_norway_bonus > 50 } }
					add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_norway_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_norway_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_allies }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.ALLIES_strength_norway_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			} else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_norway_bonus > 50 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_norway_bonus = 20 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				} else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_norway_bonus = 10 tooltip = decrease_strategic_advantage_axis }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = global.AXIS_strength_norway_bonus min = 0 max = 999 }
			}
		}
	}
	decision_theater_norway_offensive = {
		icon = theater_offensive
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = can_play_norway
		}
		available = {
			has_10_strength_norway = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = is_busy_in_theater
				NOT = {	has_decision = decision_theater_norway_retreat
						has_decision = decision_theater_norway_defend
						#has_decision = decision_theater_norway_supply
						has_decision = decision_theater_norway_reinforce }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 24.99 }
		custom_cost_text = world_stage_25_cp_cost
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 } }
		days_remove = 20 ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 15 }
			if = { limit = { has_20_strength_norway = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			if = { limit = { has_40_strength_norway = yes }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_bad = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_okk = 5 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { bonus_gud = 5 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = world_theater_country_name_self
			if = {
				limit = { has_world_stage_coalition_axis = yes }
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_norway_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_norway } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_norway_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_norway } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.AXIS_strength_norway_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_norway } }
				}
			} else = {
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_norway_bonus = bonus_bad  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_norway } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_norway_bonus = bonus_okk  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_norway } }
					1 = { add_to_variable = { global.ALLIES_strength_norway_bonus = bonus_gud  tooltip = world_stage_bonus_power_norway } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
